<Review>Cast iron sewer line and laterals in my 1959 San Diego house were shot. After getting bids from multiple companies to hydrojet then line the existing sewer lines, I called Blue Planet for a bid to pipe burst the existing lines and replace. I'm happy I decided to go with Blue Planet. Project lead Mike was great to work with and he and his assistant Yosio are incredibly hard workers. They had a great attitude, listened carefully, and also worked smoothly with the city inspector when he came to sign off on their work. At a fair price, Blue Planet replaced my original 3 inch main line with a brand new 4 inch line, and also replaced all the laterals with new pipe. They also added cleanouts on both ends of the sewer line and poured new concrete where they had to trench. After seeing the condition of the old pipes, I'm really glad I went with Blue Planet's pipe bursting approach rather than epoxy lining‚Äîwhich would have just put a veneer inside very bad pipes. Keep in mind that the pipe-bursting process is messy because you will have to dig holes on both ends of your sewer line run and anywhere you need to replace laterals. But when the work is done it's worth the temporary mess  because it's a permanent solution that gives you brand new sewer lines no matter how old your house‚Äîso reassuring to know that my wastewater problems are solved for good. I hate to report a bad experience, but I must. I told him that my drain had 32 oz of liquid drain opener in it, from my attempt to clear the clog the night before.  So when he vacuumed the water into a canister, I hoped he would be careful. <text>After placing an order for a new Corvette Z06 in January of 2017,  I had about three months to wait for it to be built and delivered.  I spent that three months researching all of the paint protection film shops in Sacramento and the Bay Area in order to find one I felt would do a good job installing paint protection film on my new car.  After contacting most of the top rated shops I could find I was surprised at how many well reviewed shops had such poor customer service.  Imperial Works was the only shop that was completely professional and thoruogh in both responding to my emails and when I spoke with them on the phone.

I received numerous quotes on the paint protection film and doing some vinyl work on my roof, and found Imperial Works pricing to be the lowest out of all the well reviewed shops I had contacted.  After speaking with one of my co-workers who had used Imperial Works several times, I finally decided that Imperial Works was the best choice.

I dropped my car off and spoke with David about what work I wanted done.  David took notes on exactly what I wanted and made numerous helpful suggestions to make sure they covered the areas of the car that were the most prone to to chips and scratches.

David and his crew corrected the factory paint then wrapped the car in XPEL.  They continually updated me with their progress and they sent me plenty pictures so I could see the application process moving along.

Upon picking up the car David went over the whole car to make sure everything was done to my satisfaction.  The car looked great and had no issues, however David made sure to let me know that I could bring the car in at any time if there was anything that was bothering me.

Well, it's been over a year since Imperial Works put the paint protection film on my car and everything still looks great.  I returned to get a stinger stripe put on my hood and a new front splitter wrapped in paint protection film.  David and his crew again did a great job and had my car done in a timely manner.

To my surprise, David had actually noticed a couple scratches in the black vinyl they put on my roof over a year ago.  The scratches were probably from the carwash, and were not David's responsibility to fix, however David completely replaced all the vinyl on my roof free of charge because he didn't want to return my car in less than perfect condition.  I noticed they also cleaned the whole exterior and shined it up for me, even though I didn't ask them to.  I have to say I am completely impressed with their work, and more importantly, that they would stand behind their work over a year later and fix things free of charge that wasn't even their fault.  I think you'd have a tough time finding a another shop anywhere that will match Imperial Works workmanship, pricing and customer service.</text><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO4fJRBWHOJlsEQ8ZAAic2Mr0k2L1g6Lj1pVDzs=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pics>< Resp>

I took my 2017 Toyota Camry into imperial works to get the windows tinted. They did an amazing job. Two days after getting them done someone smashed in my driver side window. < review>
Share review

Embed review

Write an update

Edit review

1/28/2020
My dentist for 30+ years stopped accepting my PPO insurance and I was in a panic. How would I find another dentist I  liked as well...and a hygienist? I started by asking friends and was amazed how many dentist would not accept my Blue Shield PPO. BS must have imposed a major cut on contract renewals! So I was forced to look at the list from my insurance and one by one after a visit or drive by checked them off my list until I went to check out Golden Rule Dental Center. l loved the front desk on the phone and loved everyone I met on my pop in visit. But I was still nervous about my first visit. NO NEED! My hygienist, Thomas was amazing, very thorough, understanding of my back and TMJ, issues and gets a 10+/10. He took pictures of the inside of my mouth, measured my gums and took x-rays, in addition to cleaning. He explained everything and took time to answer all my questions. Dr Kim was equally wonderful, kind and thorough. He too answered all my questions and explained everything. He even suggested a filling replacement verses a crown, which my earlier dentist had wanted to do, saving me a lot of cash. my daughter and husband will also be seeing them and I know they will agree.<//review>

<date>1604610816508< /date><rate>5< /rate>< review>
Great first experience here! A baby pigeon fell out of its nest near my house and we needed to pick up baby bird food and a feeding syringe immediately. My neighbor asked me to come by Seville Feed & Animal Supply to pick these two things up. I had never been here before but had always driven by and also had taken noticed of the stellar ratings online. I'm glad I got to experience coming here for myself!

I drove in and saw a lot of new outdoor dog houses and some other products for sale in the front of the building. I also immediately noticed a large white sign with red lettering in all caps that read, "STAY IN CAR. KEEP MASK ON". I appreciate that the staff are wearing masks and enforcing social distancing by having all customers stay in their vehicles, wear masks, and go through a drive-thru only. The staff are friendly and prompt with getting you what you need so you're in and out in no time.

A gentleman wearing a white cowboy hat and cowboy boots was friendly and professional when he approached my vehicle asking me what I needed. I got the vibe that perhaps he may have been the owner. I was there for less than five minutes and was able to the bird food and feeding syringe. I paid cash for the $13.95 total and asked them to keep the $0.05 in change. The baby bird food was $8.95 and the feeding syringe was $4.00, both very fair market price. I'm not sure if they accept credit cards but I feel like they probably prefer cash (I didn't ask).

All in all, I'm impressed! I hope to be able to visit as a walk-in customer sometime in the future once this pandemic subsides, as from what I understand, they sell baby chicks and I hope to raise my own chickens for eggs in the future. Until then, thanks, Seville Animal Feed & Supply!</review>

< Review>
Great Pizza Bad Service
Despite the bad service I've experienced the food was great.  I lived down the street and we would order our dinner at least once a week if not stop in every other week to let the kids play.  In addition we would also go for kids team pizza parties.  My experience has been that they've given my order away 2x due to placing orders on the counter and leaving it up to the customers to be honest in picking up their pizza.  Both times that this has happened to me they look at me like its my fault and after showing them my receipts and explaining to them it wasn't my fault someone got to the counter quicker than me they replaced my food but I had to wait.  In addition, on my last visit to what was my favorite pizza spot, my son and nephew were saving a table for us.  Now they were supposed to be sitting down but of course it doesn't always work that way.  My son tripped over a little girl that he didn't see laying on the floor and broke his nose on one of the benches.  All this took place inside the restaurant.  We stood there for about 10 minutes before we could get his nose to stop bleeding than I took my son to the ER.  Do you think that any of the staff came out to see if everything was ok or if there was anything that they could do to help?  Nope.  Of course all the customers around us asked if he was ok...I mean how could they not my son was crying and blood was gushing out.  But the staff...hmm...I got a bunch of stares by the young staff and I don't think the owners had a clue what was going on.  I  understand the food is great and this is a busy little spot but come on...In addition the wife, or at least I think it was the wife of the owner snapped at my husband.  She was upset because he changed his order of beer, which we had asked at the time of the order but the staff didnt make the change before she poured it.  Not our fault.  Maybe they just can't handle the stress of making money.<//Review>
